## Diagram 2

```mermaid
flowchart LR
    Start([Start]) --> GenFilename["Call __generate_filename(user_id)"]
    GenFilename --> CreateCSV["Call __create_csv_error_report(headers, rows)"]
    CreateCSV --> Check{filename and csv_report present?}
    Check -- Yes --> SaveS3["Call __save_csv_error_report(filename, csv_data)"]
    SaveS3 --> Presign["Call __generate_presigned_url(filename)"]
    Check -- No --> Presign
    Presign --> Return["Return presigned URL"]
    Return --> End([End])
    GenFilename -.->|error logged| LogError1([Log exception])
    CreateCSV -.->|error logged| LogError2([Log exception])
    SaveS3 -.->|error logged| LogError3([Log exception])
    Presign -.->|error logged| LogError4([Log exception])
```
